***нешто.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нешто.html>нешто́</a> (21174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нешто.html>не́што</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néšto</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> really?, is it possible?, indeed</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неужели.html>неуже́ли</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neužéli</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неужто.html>неу́жто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neúžto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разве.html>ра́зве</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rázve</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неэффективность.html>неэффекти́вность</a> (30484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***неяркий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неяркий.html>нея́ркий</a> (13739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:яркий.html>я́ркий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">járkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неяркий.html>нея́ркий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nejárkij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>dim, faint <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of light</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pale, impure <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of colors or sounds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> imperceptible</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> not producing a strong impression</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ordinary, nonunique</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясный.html>нея́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nejásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неясность.html>нея́сность</a> (21358)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясный.html>нея́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nejásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясность.html>нея́сность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nejásnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясность.html>нея́сности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясность.html>нея́сности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясность.html>нея́сностей</a></b>)
</p>

***ни.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> (60)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_4">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ni</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>neither, nor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ni</b> on, <b>ni</b> oná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">neither he nor she</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шает</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спи́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ni</b> kúšajet, <b>ni</b> spit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">neither eats nor sleeps</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_3">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ni</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>not a
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>ста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ni</b> odín iz sta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not one in a hundred</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(between a personal pronoun and the verb in the affirmative)</i> whatever, however
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>ска́жет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što on <b>ni</b> skážet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">whatever he says</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak by on <b>ni</b> byl bogát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">however rich he may be</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(before <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>)</i> any, no
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ге</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ni</b> v kakój kníge</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(not) in any book, in no book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>годи́тся</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ni</b> na što ne godítsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it’s good for nothing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нигде.html>нигде́</a> (2266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нигде.html>нигде́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nigdé</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nowhere
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нигде.html>нигде́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>nigdé</b> né byl</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I haven’t been anywhere.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ниже.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ниже.html>ниже́</a> (1526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nizjos</i>, which consists of <i>niz-</i> + <i>-jos</i>.
See Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">niz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ниже.html>ни́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">níže</span>) (<i>comparative of</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зкий</a>)
</p>
<ol><li>below, beneath, under</li>
<li>lower, down (from a higher to a lower position, downwards)</li>
<li>shorter</li></ol>

***нижний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нижний.html>ни́жний</a> (1632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">niz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bottom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нижний.html>ни́жний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nížnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lower, inferior
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vérxnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>under-, bottom</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***низ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низ</a> (7649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nizъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nei-ǵʰ-</i>? (Derksen) or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ni-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низ</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">niz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>ни́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bottom, lower part</li></ol>

***низкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зкий</a> (1470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nizъkъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ni-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nízkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:ниже.html>ни́же</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зший</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нижа́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>low</li>
<li>despicable</li>
<li>deep (of a sound or voice, low in frequency or pitch)</li>
<li>short (of a person)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низина.html>низи́на</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nizína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:низовой.html>низово́й</a> (24285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>низ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">niz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низовой.html>низово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nizovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lower</li>
<li>downstream, from/on the lower reaches</li>
<li>local
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низовой.html>низова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nizovája</b> organizácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>local/basic</b> organization</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низовой.html>низово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nizovój</b> rabótnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">worker in basic organization; <b>local</b> worker</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низовой.html>низова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nizovája</b> pečátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>local</b> press</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***низший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зший</a> (8908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nízšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">superlative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nízkij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">low</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>the lowest, inferior
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зшая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nízšaja</b> tóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the lowest point</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зшие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́змы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nízšije</b> organízmy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lower organisms</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зшее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>образова́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nízšeje</b> obrazovánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">primary/elementary education</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зшая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лига.html>ли́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nízšaja</b> líga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">minor league</span></div></dd>

<li>lower, subordinate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:низший.html>ни́зшая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инстанция.html>инста́нция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nízšaja</b> instáncija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lower level of authority</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***никакой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никако́й</a> (215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никако́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nikakój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(indefinite pronoun)</i> not any of possible variants, no, none; (in a negative context) whatever, whatsoever, absolutely</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (about person's state) inactive, senseless, e.g. very drunken or exhausted</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ni odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вовсе.html>во́все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vóvse ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнюдь.html>отню́дь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otnjúdʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***никитский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:никитский.html>ники́тский</a> (12369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ники́т(ский)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Nikít(skij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***никнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́кнуть</a> (15453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*niknǫti</i>. Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">vzniknout</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to arise, originate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">niknuti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sprout, spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Further cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νεῖκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neîkos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quarrel, strife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νῑ́κη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nī́kē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">victory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">níknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поникнуть.html>пони́кнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сникнуть.html>сни́кнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to droop</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***никогда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a> (207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">niekada</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nikogdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>never, nevermore <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">entails the meaning "always" or "for now on"</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лаю</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>nikogdá</b> ničevó ne délaju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I never do anything.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Sentences with the adverb <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></b> have <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in them.</li>
<li>Sentences with the adverb <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></b> have imperfective finite verbs in them. For example,</li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мила</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чашка.html>ча́шки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>nikogdá</b> ne ekonómila na čáški kófe.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have never saved on cups of coffee.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li>Using the adverb <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></b> in a sentence with a past tense shows a very strong negative. For example,</li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здила</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шади</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>nikogdá</b> ne jézdila na lóšadi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have never ridden a horse <b>at all</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kogdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">когда́-либо</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kogdá-libo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">когда́-нибудь</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kogdá-nibudʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">когда́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kogdá-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>не́когда</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nékogda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
